<div class="body yom-art-content clearfix" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/Article">         <!-- google_ad_section_start -->         <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-11-17T19:30:38Z"/>         <meta itemprop="headline" content="Parked Mercedes Racks up $22,000 in Tickets"/>         <meta itemprop="alternativeHeadline" content=""/>         <meta itemprop="image" content="https://media.zenfs.com/en-US/cms/autos/Boldride/abandoned-mercedes-1.jpg"/>         <meta itemprop="description" content="To a lover of automobiles, abandoning a car is akin to setting one’s immediate family adrift on an iceberg. It’s just plain tragic. Though not everyone shares that same feeling, and we’re guessing the owner of this forsaken Mercedes is part of that group. According to the UK’s Daily Mail, this Mercedes C-Class has sat"/>         <p><div class="yom-figure  yom-fig-xl" style="width:630px;"><a href="https://s3.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/nt6zD3WBPBvnMcPX1VT_fQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTYzMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/cms/autos/Boldride/abandoned-mercedes-1.jpg"><img class="alignnone wp-image-62472 size-full" src="https://s3.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/nt6zD3WBPBvnMcPX1VT_fQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTYzMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/cms/autos/Boldride/abandoned-mercedes-1.jpg" alt="abandoned mercedes parking garage photo" data-alt="abandoned mercedes parking garage photo" height="420" width="630"/></a></div></p> <p>To a lover of automobiles, abandoning a car is akin to setting one’s immediate family adrift on an iceberg. It’s just plain tragic. Though not everyone shares that same feeling, and we’re guessing the owner of this forsaken Mercedes is part of that group.<span id="more-62471"></span></p> <p>According to the UK’s <a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2836708/Mystery-abandoned-Mercedes-racked-14-000-car-parking-charges-three-years-multi-storey.html" target="_blank"><em>Daily Mail</em></a>, this <a href="https://autos.yahoo.com/mercedes-benz/c-class/" target="_blank">Mercedes C-Class</a> has sat abandoned in a Birmingham multi-story parking garage for three years, all the while accruing parking dues&nbsp;to the tune of about £14,000 ($22,000).</p> <p><a href="http://www.boldride.com/ride/2015/mercedes-benz-s-class-coupe" target="_blank"><strong>RELATED: The 2015 Mercedes S-Class Coupe is aggressive in all the right places</strong></a></p> <p><div class="yom-figure  yom-fig-xl" style="width:630px;"><a href="https://s3.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/ik5eKSCy_Cvz0827ZlNV.A--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTYzMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/cms/autos/Boldride/abandoned-mercedes-2.jpg"><img class="alignnone wp-image-62473 size-full" src="https://s3.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/ik5eKSCy_Cvz0827ZlNV.A--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTYzMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/cms/autos/Boldride/abandoned-mercedes-2.jpg" alt="photo of abandoned mercedes parking garage" data-alt="photo of abandoned mercedes parking garage" height="420" width="630"/></a></div></p> <p>The odd (and quite dusty) sight has drawn significant attention from regular passersby over the recent years, especially since as long as anyone can remember, it has been bookended by that safety barrier. Car park staff noted that the rear axle had significant damage, further hindering its removal process.</p> <p>Upon initial inspection, local authorities found the vehicle to be unlocked and even looked through the car’s logbook to find the driver’s details. However, attempts to locate the owner have led nowhere, and now – according to a police spokeswoman – the vehicle will finally be towed within seven days if the owner fails to be found&nbsp;again.</p> <p><a href="http://www.boldride.com/ride/2016/mercedes-amg-gt" target="_blank"><strong>PHOTOS: The stunning 2016 AMG GT is Mercedes’ biturbo V8&nbsp;rival to the Porsche 911</strong></a></p> <p><div class="yom-figure  yom-fig-xl" style="width:630px;"><a href="https://s.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/7Dv4Ooy_quYrECAlWj8BNQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTYzMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/cms/autos/Boldride/abandoned-mercedes-3.jpg"><img class="alignnone wp-image-62474 size-full" src="https://s.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/7Dv4Ooy_quYrECAlWj8BNQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTYzMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/cms/autos/Boldride/abandoned-mercedes-3.jpg" alt="abandoned mercedes parking garage photo" data-alt="abandoned mercedes parking garage photo" height="420" width="630"/></a></div></p> <p>Which we can presume he or she will try very hard not to be … as they owe the $20-a-day parking garage quite a sum of money.</p> <p><a href="http://www.boldride.com/ride/2015/mercedes-benz-s600" target="_blank"><strong>RELATED: Rule the roost in this exclusive 2015 Mercedes-Benz S600 saloon</strong></a></p> <p>________________________________________</p> <p><em>Click <a
